line=4275 tag=L:            ( of a. kaniti                gam et an independent gam et                   ha-
line=4276 tag=B:
line=4277 tag=M:             One might argue that yes is in the process of turning into a verbal element, and in that case
line=4278 tag=M:           34
line=4279 tag=B:
line=4280 tag=B:
line=4281 tag=M:  the presence of et is not surprising. There are, however, many differences between yes and real verbs,
line=4282 tag=M:  and at least one should admit that et is not restricted to lexical items that show the full inflectional
line=4283 tag=M:  paradigm of verbs. See Doron (1983) and Shlonsky (1987) for a discussion of the properties of yes.
line=4284 tag=B:
line=4285 tag=M:                                                     78
line=4286 tag=M:
line=4287 tag=M:                                                  Chapter 3: The Hebrew Object Marker et
